------- FILE i2c_v2.2.inc LEVEL 3 PASS 4
      0  1e26					      include	"i2c_v2.2.inc"
      1  1e26							;
      2  1e26							; i2c_v2.2.inc
      3  1e26							;
      4  1e26							;
      5  1e26							; AtariVox EEPROM Driver
      6  1e26							;
      7  1e26							; By Alex Herbert, 2004
      8  1e26							;
      9  1e26							; Optimisations by Thomas Jentzsch, 2006/2008
     10  1e26							;
     11  1e26
     12  1e26
     13  1e26							; I/O Constants
     14  1e26
     15  1e26		       00 04	   I2C_SDA_MASK equ	$04
     16  1e26		       00 08	   I2C_SCL_MASK equ	$08
     17  1e26
     18  1e26
     19  1e26							; Signalling Macros
     20  1e26
     21  1e26							;  MAC     I2C_SCL_0
     22  1e26							;    lda     #$00
     23  1e26							;    sta     SWCHA
     24  1e26							;  ENDM
     25  1e26
     26  1e26							;  MAC     I2C_SCL_1
     27  1e26							;    lda     #I2C_SCL_MASK
     28  1e26							;    sta     SWCHA
     29  1e26							;  ENDM
     30  1e26
     31  1e26							;  MAC     I2C_SDA_IN
     32  1e26							;    lda     #I2C_SCL_MASK
     33  1e26							;    sta     SWACNT
     34  1e26							;  ENDM
     35  1e26
     36  1e26							;  MAC     I2C_SDA_OUT
     37  1e26							;    lda     #I2C_SCL_MASK|I2C_SDA_MASK
     38  1e26							;    sta     SWACNT
     39  1e26							;  ENDM
     40  1e26
     41  1e26
     42  1e26					      MAC	i2c_start
     43  1e26							; I2C_SCL_1
     44  1e26					      lda	#(I2C_SCL_MASK|I2C_SDA_MASK)*2	; 2	     I2C_SCL_MASK
     45  1e26					      sta	SWCHA	; 4
     46  1e26							; I2C_SDA_OUT
     47  1e26					      lsr		; 2	     I2C_SCL_MASK|I2C_SDA_MASK
     48  1e26					      sta	SWACNT	; 4
     49  1e26							; total: 12 cycles
     50  1e26					      ENDM
     51  1e26
     52  1e26
     53  1e26					      MAC	i2c_txbit
     54  1e26							; I2C_SCL_0
     55  1e26					      lda	#%0011	; 2
     56  1e26					      sta	SWCHA	; 4
     57  1e26							; set bit
     58  1e26					      adc	#%1000	; 2
     59  1e26					      sta	SWACNT	; 4	     SDA = !C (a = %1000 / %1100)
     60  1e26							; I2C_SCL_1
     61  1e26					      lda	#I2C_SCL_MASK	; 2
     62  1e26					      sta	SWCHA	; 4
     63  1e26							; total: 18 cycles
     64  1e26					      ENDM
     65  1e26
     66  1e26
     67  1e26					      MAC	i2c_txnack
     68  1e26							; I2C_SCL_0
     69  1e26					      lda	#I2C_SCL_MASK*2	; 2	     $00
     70  1e26					      sta	SWCHA	; 4
     71  1e26							; I2C_SDA_IN
     72  1e26					      lsr		; 2	     I2C_SCL_MASK
     73  1e26					      sta	SWACNT	; 4
     74  1e26							; I2C_SCL_1
     75  1e26					      nop		; 2	     required for timing!
     76  1e26					      sta	SWCHA	; 4	     I2C_SCL_MASK
     77  1e26							; total: 18 cycles
     78  1e26					      ENDM
     79  1e26
     80  1e26
     81  1e26							; Subroutine Macros
     82  1e26
     83  1e26					      MAC	i2c_subs
     84  1e26
     85  1e26				   i2c_startread
     86  1e26							; use V to flag if previous byte needs ACK
     87  1e26					      ldy	#%10100001	; 2	     eeprom read command
     88  1e26					      .byte	$2c	; 2
     89  1e26				   i2c_startwrite
     90  1e26					      ldy	#%10100000	; 2	     eeprom write command
     91  1e26					      I2C_START		;12	     start signal (clears V flag)
     92  1e26					      tya		; 2 = 16
     93  1e26				   i2c_txbyte
     94  1e26					      eor	#$ff	; 2	     invert data byte
     95  1e26					      sec		; 2
     96  1e26					      rol		; 2 =	6    shift loop bit into a
     97  1e26				   i2c_txbyteloop
     98  1e26					      tay		; 2
     99  1e26					      I2C_TXBIT		;18	     transmit
    100  1e26					      tya		; 2
    101  1e26					      asl		; 2	     shift next bit into C
    102  1e26					      bne	i2c_txbyteloop	; 2= 26/27
    103  1e26
    104  1e26							; receive acknowledge bit
    105  1e26
    106  1e26					      beq	i2c_rxbit	;43 = 43
    107  1e26							; i2c_txbyte: 264 cycles
    108  1e26							;-------------------------------------------------------------------------------
    109  1e26
    110  1e26				   i2c_rxbyte
    111  1e26					      bvc	i2c_rxskipack	; 2	     previous byte needs acknowledge?
    112  1e26					      jsr	i2c_txack	;24	     transmit acknowledge bit
    113  1e26
    114  1e26				   i2c_rxskipack
    115  1e26					      bit	i2c_rxbyte	; 4	     set V - next byte(s) require acknowledge
    116  1e26
    117  1e26					      lda	#1	; 2
    118  1e26				   i2c_rxbyteloop
    119  1e26					      tay		; 2 =	2
    120  1e26				   i2c_rxbit		;	     receive bit in C
    121  1e26					      I2C_TXNACK		;18 = 18
    122  1e26
    123  1e26					      lda	SWCHA	; 4
    124  1e26					      lsr		; 2
    125  1e26					      lsr		; 2
    126  1e26					      lsr		; 2 = 10    C = SDA
    127  1e26
    128  1e26					      tya		; 2
    129  1e26					      rol		; 2	     rotate into Y
    130  1e26					      bcc	i2c_rxbyteloop	; 2=	6/7
    131  1e26
    132  1e26							; received byte in A
    133  1e26					      rts		; 6 =	6
    134  1e26							; i2c_rxbit:  40 cycles
    135  1e26							; i2c_rxbyte: 310/333 cycles
    136  1e26							;-------------------------------------------------------------------------------
    137  1e26
    138  1e26				   i2c_stopread
    139  1e26					      bvc	i2c_stopwrite	; 2
    140  1e26					      ldy	#$80	; 2
    141  1e26					      jsr	i2c_rxbit	;46	     transmit no-acknowledge
    142  1e26
    143  1e26				   i2c_stopwrite
    144  1e26					      jsr	i2c_txack	;30
    145  1e26
    146  1e26							; return port to input mode
    147  1e26					      lda	#0	; 2	     0
    148  1e26					      sta	SWACNT	; 4
    149  1e26					      rts		; 6 = 12
    150  1e26							; i2c_stopread:  45/92
    151  1e26							; i2c_stopwrite: 42
    152  1e26							;-------------------------------------------------------------------------------
    153  1e26
    154  1e26				   i2c_txack
    155  1e26							; I2C_SCL_0
    156  1e26					      lda	#0	; 2	     $00
    157  1e26					      sta	SWCHA	; 4
    158  1e26							; I2C_SDA_OUT
    159  1e26					      lda	#(I2C_SCL_MASK|I2C_SDA_MASK)	; 2	     I2C_SCL_MASK|I2C_SDA_MASK
    160  1e26					      sta	SWACNT	; 4
    161  1e26							; I2C_SCL_1
    162  1e26					      asl		; 2	     I2C_SCL_MASK
    163  1e26					      sta	SWCHA	; 4
    164  1e26
    165  1e26					      rts		; 6
    166  1e26							; total: 24 cycles
    167  1e26							;-------------------------------------------------------------------------------
    168  1e26
    169  1e26					      ENDM
    170  1e26
    171  1e26
    172  1e26

    678  1e93		       85 e2		      sta	highScoreSK+2	; 3
    679  1e95

    682  1e97		       a6 b8		      ldx	level	; 3

    692  1ea4

    695  1ea6				   .loopRead
    696  1ea6		       20 4f f6 	      jsr	i2c_rxbyte	;6+333      read byte from EEPROM
    697  1ea9		       c9 ff		      cmp	#$ff	; 2	     EEPROM slot empty?
    698  1eab		       d0 02		      bne	.skipEmpty	; 2/3	      no, skip clear
    699  1ead		       a9 00		      lda	#0	; 2	     clear EEPROM slot

      4  3f4a				  -	      ECHO	"BANK OVERFLOW @ ", * - ORIGIN

      6  3f4a					      endif

    186  4d9f							;Level element	Character	ASCII Code
    187  4d9f							;Wall	#	0x23
    188  4d9f							;Player	@	0x40
    189  4d9f							;Player on goal square	+	0x2b
    190  4d9f							;Box	$	0x24
    191  4d9f							;Box on goal square	*	0x2a
    192  4d9f							;Goal square	.	0x2e
    193  4d9f							;Floor	(Space)	0x20 or underscore
    194  4d9f
    195  4d9f							;This level ("Claire", by Lee J Haywood):
    196  4d9f
    197  4d9f							;#######
    198  4d9f							;#.@ # #
    199  4d9f							;#$* $ #
    200  4d9f							;#   $ #
    201  4d9f							;# ..	#
    202  4d9f							;#  *	#
    203  4d9f							;#######
    204  4d9f							;runlength encoded looks like this:
    205  4d9f
    206  4d9f							;The rows of the level are separated by "|"s. There has been a discussion in the Yahoo Group about what character should represent an empty square in May 2006. Finally the hyphen has been elected to be the standard character for an empty square. Nevertheless, programs are encouraged to support both, hyphens and underscores.

    208  4d9f							;If only two level elements are grouped together they may be run length encoded, but needn't to. Example:
    209  4d9f

 LEVELS6 -- full 2K (2K) SIZE =  $59f , FREE= $261
      2  4d9f					      ECHO	"LEVELS6 -- full 2K", "(2K) SIZE = ", .TEMP, ", FREE=", ROM_BANK_SIZE - .TEMP
      3  4d9f				  -	      if	( .TEMP ) > ROM_BANK_SIZE
      4  4d9f				  -	      ECHO	"BANK OVERFLOW @ ", * - ORIGIN
      5  4d9f				  -	      ERR
      6  4d9f					      endif

    165  546b
      0  546b					      CHECK_BANK_SIZE	"INITBANK"
      1  546b		       04 6b	   .TEMP      =	* - BANK_START
 INITBANK (2K) SIZE =  $46b , FREE= $395
      2  546b					      ECHO	"INITBANK", "(2K) SIZE = ", .TEMP, ", FREE=", ROM_BANK_SIZE - .TEMP
      3  546b				  -	      if	( .TEMP ) > ROM_BANK_SIZE
      4  546b				  -	      ECHO	"BANK OVERFLOW @ ", * - ORIGIN
      5  546b				  -	      ERR
      6  546b					      endif

      4  5800				   BANK_START SET	*
      5  5800				   INITBANK   SET	ORIGIN / 2048
      6  5800				   ORIGIN     SET	ORIGIN + 2048
      7  5800				   _CURRENT_BANK SET	INITBANK
     35  5800
     36  5800		       00		      .byte.b	0	; to avoid extra cycle when accessing via BoardLineStartLO-1,y
     37  5801
      0  5801					      DEFINE_SUBROUTINE	BoardLineStartLO
      1  5801		       00 0b	   BANK_BoardLineStartLO =	_CURRENT_BANK
      2  5801					      SUBROUTINE
      3  5801				   BoardLineStartLO
     39  5801
     40  5801							; Gives the start address (LO) of each board line
     41  5801					      if	1
     42  5801				   .BOARD_LOCATION SET	Board
     43  5801					      REPEAT	SIZE_BOARD_Y
     44  5801				  -	      IF	>.BOARD_LOCATION != >(.BOARD_LOCATION + SIZE_BOARD_X-1)
     45  5801				  -.BOARD_LOCATION SET	.BOARD_LOCATION - <.BOARD_LOCATION + 256
     46  5801					      ENDIF
     47  5801		       00		      .byte.b	<.BOARD_LOCATION
     48  5801				   .BOARD_LOCATION SET	.BOARD_LOCATION + SIZE_BOARD_X

    112  5843
    113  5843				   CopyROMShadowToRAM_F000
    114  5843		       a9 f0		      lda	#>$F000
    115  5845
      0  5845					      DEFINE_SUBROUTINE	CopyROMShadowToRAM	; in INITBANK
      1  5845		       00 0b	   BANK_CopyROMShadowToRAM =	_CURRENT_BANK
      2  5845					      SUBROUTINE
      3  5845				   CopyROMShadowToRAM
    117  5845
    118  5845							; Function copies a RAM prototype ROM bank into the destination RAM bank.  Typically
    119  5845							; the variable definitions are in the ROM shadow because this allows auto-initialisation
    120  5845							; of the variable contents from ROM declarations, but still allows access to them as
    121  5845							; variables when the correct RAM bank is switched in.	Code is also, of course, copied
    122  5845							; into the RAM destination so that code is callable whenever the ROM *or* RAM bank is
    123  5845							; switched in.  Further, if multiple copies are made to multiple RAM banks, then the
    124  5845							; code co-lives in all banks and may run even as bankswitching occurs between those
    125  5845							; banks -- by the very code itself.
    126  5845
    127  5845							; Note: Relies on ROM_Bank having being set via CALL mechanism to call this function
    128  5845		       85 c4		      sta	Board_AddressR+1

    942  5b09				  -	      REPEAT	10	; DIGITS 0-9
    943  5b09				  -	      .byte	<MOVE_BLANK
    944  5b09				  -	      REPEND
    945  5b09					      endif
    946  5b09
    947  5b09				  -	      if	TROPHY
    948  5b09				  -	      REPEAT	20	; 4x5
    949  5b09				  -	      .byte	<MOVE_BLANK
    950  5b09				  -	      REPEND
    951  5b09					      endif
    952  5b09
    953  5b09				  -	      IF	* - MoveVecLO != CHARACTER_MAXIMUM
    954  5b09				  -	      ECHO	"ERROR: Incorrect number of entries in MoveVecLO table!"
    955  5b09				  -	      ERR
    956  5b09					      ENDIF

      0  7858					      DEFINE_SUBROUTINE	ProcessObjStack	; 15 minimum segtime abort
      1  7858		       00 0f	   BANK_ProcessObjStack =	_CURRENT_BANK
      2  7858					      SUBROUTINE
      3  7858				   ProcessObjStack
    160  7858
    161  7858		       ad 84 02 	      lda	INTIM	;4
    162  785b		       c9 04		      cmp	#MINIMUM_SEGTIME	;2
    163  785d		       90 3b		      bcc	EarlyAbort	;2/3= 8
      0  785f					      STRESS_TIME	MINIMUM_SEGTIME
      1  785f				  -	      IF	TEST_MINIMUM_SEGTIME = 1
      2  785f				  -
      3  785f				  -
      4  785f				  -
      5  785f				  -
      6  785f				  -
      7  785f				  -	      echo	"***** WARNING! STRESS_TIME enabled @", ., "! *****"
      8  785f				  -	      bne	. - 7
      9  785f					      ENDIF
    165  785f
    166  785f		       a5 85		      lda	ObjStackNum	;3
    167  7861		       49 01		      eor	#1	;2
    168  7863		       aa		      tax		;2
    169  7864
    170  7864		       a5 d0		      lda	ObjIterator	;3
    171  7866		       d5 86		      cmp	ObjStackPtr,x	;5
    172  7868		       b0 2e		      bcs	nextPhase	;2/3
    173  786a
    174  786a
    175  786a							; Process an object...
    176  786a							; Actual object code (the handlers) starts 82 cycles after previous segtime check!
    177  786a
    178  786a		       bc 5f f9 	      ldy	BankObjStack,x	;4
    179  786d		       84 3e		      sty	SET_BANK_RAM	;3
    180  786f
    181  786f		       aa		      tax		;2
    182  7870		       bc 80 11 	      ldy	SortedObjPtr,x	;4		 indirect object pointer list (sorted)
    183  7873
    184  7873		       b9 00 10 	      lda	ObjStackX,y	;4
    185  7876		       85 8a		      sta	POS_X	;3
    186  7878		       b9 80 10 	      lda	ObjStackY,y	;4
    187  787b		       85 8b		      sta	POS_Y	;3
    188  787d		       b9 00 11 	      lda	ObjStackVar,y	;4
    189  7880		       85 8f		      sta	POS_VAR	;3
    190  7882		       be 00 12 	      ldx	ObjStackType,y	;4
    191  7885		       86 8e		      stx	POS_Type	;3
    192  7887
    193  7887		       a9 0b		      lda	#BANK_VectorProcess	;2
    194  7889		       85 3f		      sta	SET_BANK	;3
    195  788b
    196  788b		       bd fe f2 	      lda	OSPointerHI,x	;4
    197  788e		       85 de		      sta	POS_Vector+1	;3
    198  7890		       bd fd f2 	      lda	OSPointerLO,x	;4
    199  7893		       85 dd		      sta	POS_Vector	;3
    200  7895
    201  7895		       6c dd 00 	      jmp	(POS_Vector)	;5 = 82	 vector to processor for particular object type
    202  7898
    203  7898
    204  7898							;---------------------------------------------------------------------------
    205  7898							; Now process the blank stack.  This stack holds all the recently blanked squares
    206  7898							; and determines (and moves) BOXs or TARGETs into these squares.  The space vacated
    207  7898							; by these objects are added again to the blank stack.
    208  7898
    209  7898				   nextPhase
    210  7898
    211  7898							;clc
    212  7898							;lda circle_d
    213  7898							;adc #255
    214  7898							;sta circle_d
    215  7898							;bcc nocirc
    216  7898							;nocirc
    217  7898
    218  7898		       e6 89		      inc	ScreenDrawPhase	;5		 obj/blank finished -- let the draw stuff proceed
    219  789a		       60	   EarlyAbort rts		;6
    220  789b
    221  789b							;---------------------------------------------------------------------------
    222  789b
      0  789b					      DEFINE_SUBROUTINE	SwitchObjects	;=72
      1  789b		       00 0f	   BANK_SwitchObjects =	_CURRENT_BANK
      2  789b					      SUBROUTINE
      3  789b				   SwitchObjects
    224  789b
    225  789b							; The game loop has come to an end. The only possible "still happening" thing is the sort, which runs
    226  789b							; in parallel with other processes (objects, draw stack, etc). We may or may not want to wait for the
    227  789b							; sort to complete.  This code does all the checks needed to switch to the next game frame.
    228  789b
    229  789b		       ad 84 02 	      lda	INTIM	; 4
    230  789e		       c9 02		      cmp	#SEGTIME_SWITCHOBJECTS	; 2
    231  78a0		       90 f8		      bcc	EarlyAbort	; 2/3= 8
      0  78a2					      STRESS_TIME	SEGTIME_SWITCHOBJECTS
      1  78a2				  -	      IF	TEST_SEGTIME_SWITCHOBJECTS = 1
      2  78a2				  -
      3  78a2				  -
      4  78a2				  -
      5  78a2				  -
      6  78a2				  -
      7  78a2				  -	      echo	"***** WARNING! STRESS_TIME enabled @", ., "! *****"
      8  78a2				  -	      bne	. - 7
      9  78a2					      ENDIF
    233  78a2
    234  78a2							; If we're undertime, then abort. The sort will continue to run, and that's great. Only when
    235  78a2							; we're at the throttle cutoff do we switch game-frames.
    236  78a2
    237  78a2							;sec
    238  78a2		       a5 ba		      lda	Throttle	;3
    239  78a4		       e9 a0		      sbc	#MAX_THROTTLE	;2
    240  78a6		       90 f2		      bcc	EarlyAbort	;2/3		 plenty of time left!
    241  78a8
    242  78a8							; Time is up. But we may be in a level which requires perfect sorting
    243  78a8							; So we check for these levels, and wait for the sort to complete for those.
    244  78a8
    245  78a8		       24 b9		      bit	levelDisplay	;3
    246  78aa		       50 08		      bvc	keepFractional	;2/3		 screen does not require complete sort
    247  78ac
    248  78ac							; We have a level which requires the sort to go to completion
    249  78ac							; Check to see if the sort is finished...
    250  78ac
    251  78ac		       a4 cf		      ldy	sortPtr	;3
    252  78ae		       d0 ea		      bne	EarlyAbort	;2/3		 sort still in progress, so wait
    253  78b0		       a4 ce		      ldy	sortRequired	;3
    254  78b2		       10 e6		      bpl	EarlyAbort	;2/3		 sort still in progress, so wait
    255  78b4
    256  78b4		       85 ba	   keepFractional sta	Throttle	;3		 save fractional 'left over' bit
    257  78b6
    258  78b6							; Pause the game with B/W switch:
    259  78b6
    260  78b6		       a5 80		      lda	gameMode
    261  78b8		       30 14		      bmi	.paused	; pause flag set
    262  78ba
    263  78ba							; Now that we have completed processing the object stack, we switch
    264  78ba							; the stack bank pointers for the next time around.
    265  78ba
    266  78ba		       a5 85		      lda	ObjStackNum	;3
    267  78bc		       49 01		      eor	#1	;2
    268  78be		       aa		      tax		;2
    269  78bf		       86 85		      stx	ObjStackNum	;3		 swap stacks @here
    270  78c1
    271  78c1							; STOP the sort so it doesn't corrupt the "other" object stack. Sort may get a look-in immediately after
    272  78c1							; this code is finished, so we don't want it to do something unexpected!
    273  78c1
    274  78c1		       a0 ff		      ldy	#<(-1)	;2
    275  78c3		       84 ce		      sty	sortRequired	;3
    276  78c5		       c8		      iny		;2		 Y==0
    277  78c6		       84 cf		      sty	sortPtr	;3
    278  78c8
    279  78c8							; Initialise the iterator and stack pointer for next time around.
    280  78c8							; Previously the stack pointer auto-initialised by popping the stack. Now we have an iterator it's
    281  78c8							; necessary to initialise both.
    282  78c8
    283  78c8		       84 d0		      sty	ObjIterator	;3		 Y==0
    284  78ca		       94 86		      sty	ObjStackPtr,x	;4
    285  78cc
    286  78cc		       84 89		      sty	ScreenDrawPhase	;3
    287  78ce				   .paused
    288  78ce		       60	   quickExit  rts		;6
    289  78cf
    290  78cf							;---------------------------------------------------------------------------
    291  78cf
    292  78cf				  -	      if	0
    293  78cf				  -	      DEFINE_SUBROUTINE	PROCESS_CIRCLE_DRAWER
    294  78cf				  -
    295  78cf				  -	      ldy	#CHARACTER_BLANK
    296  78cf				  -	      lda	circle_d+1
    297  78cf				  -			;jsr DrawCircle
    298  78cf				  -			;bcc finCircle
    299  78cf				  -			;lda #TYPE_CIRCLE_DRAWER
    300  78cf				  -			;sta POS_Type
    301  78cf				  -			;jsr InsertObjectStack
    302  78cf				  -finCircle  jmp	NextObject
    303  78cf				  -
    304  78cf				  -	      DEFINE_SUBROUTINE	PROCESS_CIRCLE_HELPER
    305  78cf				  -
    306  78cf				  -	      lda	INTIM
    307  78cf				  -	      cmp	#SEGTIME_CIRCLE_HELPER
    308  78cf				  -	      bcc	EarlyAbort
    309  78cf				  -
    310  78cf				  -
    311  78cf				  -	      jmp	NextObject	; and die
    312  78cf				  -
    313  78cf				  -
    314  78cf				  -	      DEFINE_SUBROUTINE	PROCESS_CIRCLE
    315  78cf				  -
    316  78cf				  -	      lda	INTIM
    317  78cf				  -	      cmp	#SEGTIME_CIRCLE
    318  78cf				  -	      bcc	EarlyAbort
    319  78cf				  -
    320  78cf				  -	      clc
    321  78cf				  -	      lda	circle_d
    322  78cf				  -	      adc	#255
    323  78cf				  -	      sta	circle_d
    324  78cf				  -	      bcc	inactiveCircle
    325  78cf				  -
    326  78cf				  -	      inc	circle_d+1
    327  78cf				  -	      lda	circle_d+1
    328  78cf				  -	      cmp	#20
    329  78cf				  -	      beq	circleComplete
    330  78cf				  -			; time to fire off another "ring" of the clearing circle

      0  7a1b					      DEFINE_SUBROUTINE	TimeSlice
      1  7a1b		       00 0f	   BANK_TimeSlice =	_CURRENT_BANK
      2  7a1b					      SUBROUTINE
      3  7a1b				   TimeSlice
    710  7a1b
    711  7a1b							; FIRST check the time is sufficient for the smallest of the timeslices. Not much point
    712  7a1b							; going ahead if there's insufficient time. This allows the previous character drawing to
    713  7a1b							; be much smaller in time, as they don't have to include the timeslice code overhead.
    714  7a1b
    715  7a1b		       ad 84 02 	      lda	INTIM	; 4
    716  7a1e		       c9 05		      cmp	#SEGTIME_MINIMUM_TIMESLICE	; 2
    717  7a20		       90 b4		      bcc	timeExit	; 2(3)
    718  7a22
    719  7a22							; Uses the phase variable to vector to the correct processing code for the given timeslice
    720  7a22							; Code may be in any bank. Avoid the fixed bank at all costs!	Once a section is complete
    721  7a22							; it should increment ScreenDrawPhase.
    722  7a22
    723  7a22							; Switched-in bank(s) are undefined after this function is called!
    724  7a22
    725  7a22		       a9 03		      lda	#BANK_TS_PhaseVectorLO	; 2
    726  7a24		       85 3f		      sta	SET_BANK	; 3
    727  7a26
    728  7a26		       a6 89		      ldx	ScreenDrawPhase	; 3		 current phase of drawing
    729  7a28		       bd 49 f5 	      lda	TS_PhaseVectorLO,x	; 4
    730  7a2b		       85 dd		      sta	TS_Vector	; 3
    731  7a2d		       bd 4e f5 	      lda	TS_PhaseVectorHI,x	; 4
    732  7a30		       85 de		      sta	TS_Vector+1	; 3
    733  7a32
    734  7a32		       bd 53 f5 	      lda	TS_PhaseBank,x	; 4
    735  7a35		       85 3f		      sta	SET_BANK	; 3		 switch bank
    736  7a37

------- FILE sound/intro1_player.asm LEVEL 3 PASS 4
      0  7b48					      include	"sound/intro1_player.asm"
      1  7b48							; TIATracker music player
      2  7b48							; Copyright 2016 Andre "Kylearan" Wichmann
      3  7b48							; Website: https://bitbucket.org/kylearan/tiatracker
      4  7b48							; Email: andre.wichmann@gmx.de
      5  7b48							;
      6  7b48							; Licensed under the Apache License, Version 2.0 (the "License");
      7  7b48							; you may not use this file except in compliance with the License.
      8  7b48							; You may obtain a copy of the License at
      9  7b48							;
     10  7b48							;   http://www.apache.org/licenses/LICENSE-2.0
     11  7b48							;
     12  7b48							; Unless required by applicable law or agreed to in writing, software
     13  7b48							; distributed under the License is distributed on an "AS IS" BASIS,
     14  7b48							; WITHOUT WARRANTIES OR CONDITIONS OF ANY KIND, either express or implied.
     15  7b48							; See the License for the specific language governing permissions and
     16  7b48							; limitations under the License.
     17  7b48
     18  7b48							; Song author: 
     19  7b48							; Song name: 
     20  7b48
     21  7b48							; @com.wudsn.ide.asm.hardware=ATARI2600
     22  7b48
     23  7b48							; =====================================================================
     24  7b48							; TIATracker Player
     25  7b48							; =====================================================================
     26  7b48				   tt_PlayerStart
     27  7b48
     28  7b48							; PLANNED PLAYER VARIANTS:
     29  7b48							; - RAM, speed, player ROM: c0/c1 patterns have same length
     30  7b48							; - RAM: Pack 2 values (out of cur_pat_index, cur_note_index, envelope_index)
     31  7b48							;	 into one and use lsr/asl to unpack them, allowing only ranges of
     32  7b48							;	 16/16 or 32/8 for them, depending on number of patterns, max
     33  7b48							;	 pattern size and max ADSR size
     34  7b48							; - ROM: Check if tt_SequenceTable can hold ptrs directly without indexing
     35  7b48							;	 tt_PatternPtrLo/Hi. Can be smaller if not many patterns get repeated
     36  7b48							;	 (saves table and decode routine)
     37  7b48							; - Speed: Inline tt_CalcInsIndex
     38  7b48							; - Speed: Store ptr to current note in RAM instead of reconstructing it?
     39  7b48							;	 Might also save the need for cur_note_index
     40  7b48
     41  7b48
     42  7b48							; ---------------------------------------------------------------------
     43  7b48							; Helper macro: Retrieves current note. May advance pattern if needed.
     44  7b48							; Becomes a subroutine if TT_USE_OVERLAY is used.
     45  7b48							; ---------------------------------------------------------------------
     46  7b48					      MAC	tt_fetch_current_note
     47  7b48							; construct ptr to pattern
     48  7b48				   .constructPatPtr
     49  7b48					      ldy	tt_cur_pat_index_c0,x	; get current pattern (index into tt_SequenceTable)
     50  7b48					      lda	tt_SequenceTable,y
     51  7b48					      IF	TT_USE_GOTO = 1
     52  7b48					      bpl	.noPatternGoto
     53  7b48					      and	#%01111111	; mask out goto bit to get pattern number
     54  7b48					      sta	tt_cur_pat_index_c0,x	; store goto'ed pattern index
     55  7b48					      bpl	.constructPatPtr	; unconditional
     56  7b48				   .noPatternGoto
     57  7b48					      ENDIF
     58  7b48					      tay
     59  7b48					      lda	tt_PatternPtrLo,y
     60  7b48					      sta	tt_ptr
     61  7b48					      lda	tt_PatternPtrHi,y
     62  7b48					      sta	tt_ptr+1
     63  7b48							; get new note
     64  7b48					      IF	TT_USE_OVERLAY = 0
     65  7b48					      ldy	tt_cur_note_index_c0,x
     66  7b48					      ELSE
     67  7b48							; If the V flag is set and if the new note is an instrument,
     68  7b48							; it means it got pre-fetched by an overlay percussion, it has
     69  7b48							; to remain in sustain.
     70  7b48					      clv
     71  7b48							; check if note had been pre-fetched by overlay perc already
     72  7b48					      lda	tt_cur_note_index_c0,x
     73  7b48					      bpl	.notPrefetched
     74  7b48							; If so, remove flag
     75  7b48					      and	#%01111111
     76  7b48					      sta	tt_cur_note_index_c0,x
     77  7b48							; Set V flag for later
     78  7b48					      bit	tt_Bit6Set
     79  7b48				   .notPrefetched
     80  7b48					      tay
     81  7b48					      ENDIF
     82  7b48					      lda	(tt_ptr),y
     83  7b48							; pre-process new note
     84  7b48							; 7..5: instrument (1..7), 4..0 (0..31): frequency
     85  7b48							; 0/0: End of pattern
     86  7b48					      bne	.noEndOfPattern
     87  7b48							; End of pattern: Advance to next pattern
     88  7b48					      sta	tt_cur_note_index_c0,x	; a is 0
     89  7b48					      inc	tt_cur_pat_index_c0,x
     90  7b48					      bne	.constructPatPtr	; unconditional
     91  7b48				   .noEndOfPattern
     92  7b48					      ENDM
     93  7b48
     94  7b48
     95  7b48							; ---------------------------------------------------------------------
     96  7b48							; Music player entry. Call once per frame.
     97  7b48							; ---------------------------------------------------------------------
     98  7b48				   tt_Player  SUBROUTINE
     99  7b48							; ==================== Sequencer ====================
    100  7b48							; Decrease speed timer
    101  7b48		       c6 d2		      dec	tt_timer
    102  7b4a		       10 6e		      bpl	.noNewNote
    103  7b4c
    104  7b4c							; Timer ran out: Do sequencer
    105  7b4c							; Advance to next note
    106  7b4c		       a2 01		      ldx	#1	; 2 channels
    107  7b4e				   .advanceLoop
    108  7b4e					      IF	TT_USE_OVERLAY = 1
    109  7b4e		       20 64 fb 	      jsr	tt_FetchNote
    110  7b51				  -	      ELSE
    111  7b51				  -	      TT_FETCH_CURRENT_NOTE
    112  7b51					      ENDIF
    113  7b51							; Parse new note from pattern
    114  7b51		       c9 10		      cmp	#TT_INS_PAUSE
    115  7b53					      IF	TT_USE_SLIDE = 0
    116  7b53		       90 55		      bcc	.finishedNewNote
    117  7b55		       d0 3d		      bne	.newNote
    118  7b57				  -	      ELSE
    119  7b57				  -	      beq	.pause
    120  7b57				  -	      bcs	.newNote
    121  7b57				  -
    122  7b57				  -			; --- slide/hold ---
    123  7b57				  -			; Adjust frequency and hold note in sustain.
    124  7b57				  -			; composer/tracker has to make sure that no unwanted
    125  7b57				  -			; under/overflow happens.
    126  7b57				  -			; Note: f = f + (8-(16-x)) = x + f - 8
    127  7b57				  -	      adc	tt_cur_ins_c0,x	; carry is clear after cmp
    128  7b57				  -	      sec
    129  7b57				  -	      sbc	#8
    130  7b57				  -	      sta	tt_cur_ins_c0,x
    131  7b57				  -	      bcs	.finishedNewNote	; unconditional, since legally no underflow can happen (ins>0 or HOLD for ins=0)
    132  7b57					      ENDIF
    133  7b57
    134  7b57							; --- pause ---
    135  7b57				   .pause
    136  7b57							; Get release index for current instrument. Since a pause can
    137  7b57							; only follow an instrument, we don't need to handle percussion
    138  7b57							; or commands.
    139  7b57		       b5 d9		      lda	tt_cur_ins_c0,x
    140  7b59		       20 f2 fb 	      jsr	tt_CalcInsIndex
    141  7b5c		       b9 b0 fc 	      lda	tt_InsReleaseIndexes-1,y	; -1 b/c instruments start at #1
    142  7b5f							; Put it into release. Skip junk byte so index no longer indicates
    143  7b5f							; sustain phase.
    144  7b5f		       18		      clc
    145  7b60		       69 01		      adc	#1
    146  7b62		       90 44		      bcc	.storeADIndex	; unconditional
    147  7b64
    148  7b64							; ---------------------------------------------------------------------
    149  7b64							; Helper subroutine to minimize ROM footprint. Will be inlined if
    150  7b64							; TT_USE_OVERLAY is not used.
    151  7b64							; Interleaved here so player can be inlined.
    152  7b64							; ---------------------------------------------------------------------
    153  7b64					      IF	TT_USE_OVERLAY = 1
    154  7b64				   tt_FetchNote
      0  7b64					      TT_FETCH_CURRENT_NOTE
      1  7b64
      2  7b64				   .constructPatPtr
      3  7b64		       b4 d3		      ldy	tt_cur_pat_index_c0,x
      4  7b66		       b9 c3 fd 	      lda	tt_SequenceTable,y
      5  7b69					      IF	TT_USE_GOTO = 1
      6  7b69		       10 06		      bpl	.noPatternGoto
      7  7b6b		       29 7f		      and	#%01111111
      8  7b6d		       95 d3		      sta	tt_cur_pat_index_c0,x
      9  7b6f		       10 f3		      bpl	.constructPatPtr
     10  7b71				   .noPatternGoto
     11  7b71					      ENDIF
     12  7b71		       a8		      tay
     13  7b72		       b9 b9 fd 	      lda	tt_PatternPtrLo,y
     14  7b75		       85 db		      sta	tt_ptr
     15  7b77		       b9 be fd 	      lda	tt_PatternPtrHi,y
     16  7b7a		       85 dc		      sta	tt_ptr+1
     17  7b7c
     18  7b7c				  -	      IF	TT_USE_OVERLAY = 0
     19  7b7c				  -	      ldy	tt_cur_note_index_c0,x
     20  7b7c					      ELSE
     21  7b7c
     22  7b7c
     23  7b7c
     24  7b7c		       b8		      clv
     25  7b7d
     26  7b7d		       b5 d5		      lda	tt_cur_note_index_c0,x
     27  7b7f		       10 07		      bpl	.notPrefetched
     28  7b81
     29  7b81		       29 7f		      and	#%01111111
     30  7b83		       95 d5		      sta	tt_cur_note_index_c0,x
     31  7b85
     32  7b85		       2c f8 fb 	      bit	tt_Bit6Set
     33  7b88				   .notPrefetched
     34  7b88		       a8		      tay
     35  7b89					      ENDIF
     36  7b89		       b1 db		      lda	(tt_ptr),y
     37  7b8b
     38  7b8b
     39  7b8b
     40  7b8b		       d0 06		      bne	.noEndOfPattern
     41  7b8d
     42  7b8d		       95 d5		      sta	tt_cur_note_index_c0,x
     43  7b8f		       f6 d3		      inc	tt_cur_pat_index_c0,x
     44  7b91		       d0 d1		      bne	.constructPatPtr
     45  7b93				   .noEndOfPattern
    156  7b93		       60		      rts
    157  7b94					      ENDIF
    158  7b94
    159  7b94
    160  7b94							; --- start instrument or percussion ---
    161  7b94				   .newNote
    162  7b94		       95 d9		      sta	tt_cur_ins_c0,x	; set new instrument
    163  7b96							; Instrument or percussion?
    164  7b96		       c9 20		      cmp	#TT_FREQ_MASK+1
    165  7b98		       b0 06		      bcs	.startInstrument
    166  7b9a
    167  7b9a							; --- start percussion ---
    168  7b9a							; Get index of envelope
    169  7b9a		       a8		      tay
    170  7b9b							; -TT_FIRST_PERC because percussion start with TT_FIRST_PERC
    171  7b9b		       b9 d4 fc 	      lda	tt_PercIndexes-TT_FIRST_PERC,y
    172  7b9e		       d0 08		      bne	.storeADIndex	; unconditional, since index values are >0
    173  7ba0
    174  7ba0							; --- start instrument ---
    175  7ba0				   .startInstrument
    176  7ba0					      IF	TT_USE_OVERLAY = 1
    177  7ba0							; If V flag is set, this note had been pre-fetched. That means
    178  7ba0							; it should remain in sustain.
    179  7ba0		       70 08		      bvs	.finishedNewNote
    180  7ba2					      ENDIF
    181  7ba2							; Put note into attack/decay
    182  7ba2		       20 f2 fb 	      jsr	tt_CalcInsIndex
    183  7ba5		       b9 a6 fc 	      lda	tt_InsADIndexes-1,y	; -1 because instruments start at #1
    184  7ba8				   .storeADIndex
    185  7ba8		       95 d7		      sta	tt_envelope_index_c0,x
    186  7baa
    187  7baa							; --- Finished parsing new note ---
    188  7baa				   .finishedNewNote
    189  7baa							; increase note index into pattern
    190  7baa		       f6 d5		      inc	tt_cur_note_index_c0,x
    191  7bac							; loop over channels
    192  7bac				   .sequencerNextChannel
    193  7bac		       ca		      dex
    194  7bad		       10 9f		      bpl	.advanceLoop
    195  7baf
    196  7baf							; Reset timer value
    197  7baf				  -	      IF	TT_GLOBAL_SPEED = 0
    198  7baf				  -			; Get timer value for current pattern in channel 0
    199  7baf				  -	      ldx	tt_cur_pat_index_c0	; get current pattern (index into tt_SequenceTable)
    200  7baf				  -	      ldy	tt_SequenceTable,x	; Current pattern index now in y
    201  7baf				  -	      IF	TT_USE_FUNKTEMPO = 0
    202  7baf				  -	      lda	tt_PatternSpeeds,y
    203  7baf				  -	      sta	tt_timer
    204  7baf				  -	      ELSE
    205  7baf				  -			; Test for odd/even frame
    206  7baf				  -	      lda	tt_cur_note_index_c0
    207  7baf				  -	      lsr
    208  7baf				  -	      lda	tt_PatternSpeeds,y	; does not affect carry flag
    209  7baf				  -	      bcc	.evenFrame
    210  7baf				  -	      and	#$0f	; does not affect carry flag
    211  7baf				  -	      bcs	.storeFunkTempo
    212  7baf				  -.evenFrame
    213  7baf				  -	      lsr
    214  7baf				  -	      lsr
    215  7baf				  -	      lsr
    216  7baf				  -	      lsr
    217  7baf				  -.storeFunkTempo
    218  7baf				  -	      sta	tt_timer
    219  7baf				  -	      ENDIF		; TT_USE_FUNKTEMPO = 0
    220  7baf				  -
    221  7baf					      ELSE
    222  7baf							; Global tempo
    223  7baf		       a2 04		      ldx	#TT_SPEED-1
    224  7bb1					      IF	TT_USE_FUNKTEMPO = 1
    225  7bb1		       a5 d5		      lda	tt_cur_note_index_c0
    226  7bb3		       4a		      lsr
    227  7bb4		       90 02		      bcc	.noOddFrame
    228  7bb6		       a2 03		      ldx	#TT_ODD_SPEED-1
    229  7bb8				   .noOddFrame
    230  7bb8					      ENDIF		; TT_USE_FUNKTEMPO = 1
    231  7bb8		       86 d2		      stx	tt_timer
    232  7bba					      ENDIF		; TT_GLOBAL_SPEED = 0
    233  7bba
    234  7bba							; No new note to process
    235  7bba				   .noNewNote
    236  7bba
    237  7bba							; ==================== Update registers ====================
    238  7bba		       a2 01		      ldx	#1	; 2 channels
    239  7bbc				   .updateLoop
    240  7bbc							; Percussion or melodic instrument?
    241  7bbc		       b5 d9		      lda	tt_cur_ins_c0,x
    242  7bbe				  -	      IF	TT_STARTS_WITH_NOTES = 0
    243  7bbe				  -			; This branch can be removed if track starts with a note in each channel
    244  7bbe				  -	      beq	.afterAudioUpdate
    245  7bbe					      ENDIF
    246  7bbe		       c9 20		      cmp	#TT_FREQ_MASK+1
    247  7bc0		       b0 37		      bcs	.instrument	; Melodic instrument
    248  7bc2
    249  7bc2							; --- Percussion: Get envelope index ---
    250  7bc2		       b4 d7		      ldy	tt_envelope_index_c0,x
    251  7bc4							; Set AUDC and AUDV value from envelope
    252  7bc4		       b9 fd fc 	      lda	tt_PercCtrlVolTable-1,y	; -1 because values are stored +1
    253  7bc7		       f0 02		      beq	.endOfPercussion	; 0 means end of percussion data
    254  7bc9		       f6 d7		      inc	tt_envelope_index_c0,x	; if end not reached: advance index
    255  7bcb				   .endOfPercussion
    256  7bcb		       95 59		      sta	AUDV0,x
    257  7bcd		       4a		      lsr
    258  7bce		       4a		      lsr
    259  7bcf		       4a		      lsr
    260  7bd0		       4a		      lsr
    261  7bd1		       95 55		      sta	AUDC0,x
    262  7bd3							; Set AUDF
    263  7bd3		       b9 e7 fc 	      lda	tt_PercFreqTable-1,y	; -1 because values are stored +1
    264  7bd6							; Bit 7 (overlay) might be set, but is unused in AUDF
    265  7bd6		       95 57		      sta	AUDF0,x
    266  7bd8					      IF	TT_USE_OVERLAY = 1
    267  7bd8		       10 48		      bpl	.afterAudioUpdate
    268  7bda							; Overlay percussion: Fetch next note out of order
    269  7bda		       20 64 fb 	      jsr	tt_FetchNote
    270  7bdd							; Only do something if it's a melodic instrument
    271  7bdd		       c9 20		      cmp	#TT_FREQ_MASK+1
    272  7bdf		       90 41		      bcc	.afterAudioUpdate
    273  7be1							; Instrument: Put into sustain
    274  7be1		       95 d9		      sta	tt_cur_ins_c0,x	; set new instrument
    275  7be3		       20 f2 fb 	      jsr	tt_CalcInsIndex
    276  7be6		       b9 ab fc 	      lda	tt_InsSustainIndexes-1,y	; -1 because instruments start at #1
    277  7be9		       95 d7		      sta	tt_envelope_index_c0,x
    278  7beb							; Set prefetch flag. asl-sec-ror is smaller than lda-ora #128-sta
    279  7beb		       16 d5		      asl	tt_cur_note_index_c0,x
    280  7bed		       38		      sec
    281  7bee		       76 d5		      ror	tt_cur_note_index_c0,x
    282  7bf0		       30 30		      bmi	.afterAudioUpdate	; unconditional
    283  7bf2				  -	      ELSE
    284  7bf2				  -	      jmp	.afterAudioUpdate
    285  7bf2					      ENDIF
    286  7bf2
    287  7bf2
    288  7bf2							; ---------------------------------------------------------------------
    289  7bf2							; Helper subroutine to minimize ROM footprint.
    290  7bf2							; Interleaved here so player routine can be inlined.
    291  7bf2							; ---------------------------------------------------------------------
    292  7bf2				   tt_CalcInsIndex
    293  7bf2							; move upper 3 bits to lower 3
    294  7bf2		       4a		      lsr
    295  7bf3		       4a		      lsr
    296  7bf4		       4a		      lsr
    297  7bf5		       4a		      lsr
    298  7bf6		       4a		      lsr
    299  7bf7		       a8		      tay
    300  7bf8				   tt_Bit6Set		; This opcode has bit #6 set, for use with bit instruction
    301  7bf8		       60		      rts
    302  7bf9
    303  7bf9
    304  7bf9				   .instrument
    305  7bf9							; --- Melodic instrument ---
    306  7bf9							; Compute index into ADSR indexes and master Ctrl tables
    307  7bf9		       20 f2 fb 	      jsr	tt_CalcInsIndex
    308  7bfc							; Set AUDC with master value for this instrument, while we are at it
    309  7bfc		       b9 a1 fc 	      lda	tt_InsCtrlTable-1,y	; -1 because instruments start with #1
    310  7bff		       95 55		      sta	AUDC0,x
    311  7c01							; advance ADSR counter and compare to end of Sustain
    312  7c01		       b5 d7		      lda	tt_envelope_index_c0,x
    313  7c03		       d9 b0 fc 	      cmp	tt_InsReleaseIndexes-1,y	; -1 because instruments start with #1
    314  7c06		       d0 03		      bne	.noEndOfSustain
    315  7c08							; End of sustain: Go back to start of sustain
    316  7c08		       b9 ab fc 	      lda	tt_InsSustainIndexes-1,y	; -1 because instruments start with #1
    317  7c0b				   .noEndOfSustain
    318  7c0b		       a8		      tay
    319  7c0c							; Set volume from envelope
    320  7c0c		       b9 b6 fc 	      lda	tt_InsFreqVolTable,y
    321  7c0f		       f0 01		      beq	.endOfEnvelope	; 0 means end of release has been reached:
    322  7c11		       c8		      iny		; advance index otherwise
    323  7c12				   .endOfEnvelope
    324  7c12		       94 d7		      sty	tt_envelope_index_c0,x
    325  7c14		       95 59		      sta	AUDV0,x
    326  7c16							; Now adjust frequency with ADSR value from envelope
    327  7c16		       4a		      lsr
    328  7c17		       4a		      lsr
    329  7c18		       4a		      lsr
    330  7c19		       4a		      lsr
    331  7c1a		       18		      clc
    332  7c1b		       75 d9		      adc	tt_cur_ins_c0,x
    333  7c1d		       38		      sec
    334  7c1e		       e9 08		      sbc	#8
    335  7c20		       95 57		      sta	AUDF0,x
    336  7c22
    337  7c22				   .afterAudioUpdate
    338  7c22							; loop over channels
    339  7c22		       ca		      dex
    340  7c23		       10 97		      bpl	.updateLoop
    341  7c25
 Music player size:  $dd

      2  7c86					      SUBROUTINE
      3  7c86				   switchLevels
   1183  7c86
   1184  7c86							;lda #BANK_NextLevelX
   1185  7c86							;sta SET_BANK
   1186  7c86							;jmp NextLevelX
   1187  7c86
   1188  7c86							; Now do the actual switching
   1189  7c86
   1190  7c86		       a5 cd		      lda	NextLevelTrigger
   1191  7c88		       29 7f		      and	#<(~BIT_NEXTLEVEL)
   1192  7c8a		       85 cd		      sta	NextLevelTrigger
   1193  7c8c
   1194  7c8c							; Next level is due. Point to the next level, but if we're at the end of playable levels,
   1195  7c8c							; then increment the level number. This is completely circular, so we eventually wrap
   1196  7c8c							; the level back to 0 and start afresh.
   1197  7c8c
   1198  7c8c		       e6 b7		      inc	levelX
   1199  7c8e		       a5 b7		      lda	levelX
   1200  7c90		       c9 9e		      cmp	#MAX_LEVEL_NUMBER
   1201  7c92		       90 02		      bcc	.level_ok
   1202  7c94		       a9 00		      lda	#0
   1203  7c96		       85 b7	   .level_ok  sta	levelX
   1204  7c98		       60		      rts

     23  7ca2							; =====================================================================
     24  7ca2							; TIATracker melodic and percussion instruments, patterns and sequencer
     25  7ca2							; data.
     26  7ca2							; =====================================================================
     27  7ca2				   tt_TrackDataStart
     28  7ca2
     29  7ca2							; =====================================================================
     30  7ca2							; Melodic instrument definitions (up to 7). tt_envelope_index_c0/1 hold
     31  7ca2							; the index values into these tables for the current instruments played
     32  7ca2							; in channel 0 and 1.
     33  7ca2							; 
     34  7ca2							; Each instrument is defined by:
     35  7ca2							; - tt_InsCtrlTable: the AUDC value
     36  7ca2							; - tt_InsADIndexes: the index of the start of the ADSR envelope as
     37  7ca2							;	 defined in tt_InsFreqVolTable
     38  7ca2							; - tt_InsSustainIndexes: the index of the start of the Sustain phase
     39  7ca2							;	 of the envelope
     40  7ca2							; - tt_InsReleaseIndexes: the index of the start of the Release phase
     41  7ca2							; - tt_InsFreqVolTable: The AUDF frequency and AUDV volume values of
     42  7ca2							;	 the envelope
     43  7ca2							; =====================================================================
     44  7ca2
     45  7ca2							; Instrument master CTRL values
     46  7ca2				   tt_InsCtrlTable
     47  7ca2		       07 04 0c 04*	      dc.b	$07, $04, $0c, $04, $0c
     48  7ca7
     49  7ca7
     50  7ca7							; Instrument Attack/Decay start indexes into ADSR tables.
     51  7ca7				   tt_InsADIndexes
     52  7ca7		       00 0e 0e 1e*	      dc.b	$00, $0e, $0e, $1e, $1e
     53  7cac
     54  7cac
     55  7cac							; Instrument Sustain start indexes into ADSR tables
     56  7cac				   tt_InsSustainIndexes
     57  7cac		       08 19 19 2b*	      dc.b	$08, $19, $19, $2b, $2b
     58  7cb1
     59  7cb1
     60  7cb1							; Instrument Release start indexes into ADSR tables
     61  7cb1							; Caution: Values are stored with an implicit -1 modifier! To get the
     62  7cb1							; real index, add 1.
     63  7cb1				   tt_InsReleaseIndexes
     64  7cb1		       09 1b 1b 2c*	      dc.b	$09, $1b, $1b, $2c, $2c
     65  7cb6
     66  7cb6
     67  7cb6							; AUDVx and AUDFx ADSR envelope values.
     68  7cb6							; Each byte encodes the frequency and volume:
     69  7cb6							; - Bits 7..4: Freqency modifier for the current note ([-8..7]),
     70  7cb6							;	 8 means no change. Bit 7 is the sign bit.
     71  7cb6							; - Bits 3..0: Volume
     72  7cb6							; Between sustain and release is one byte that is not used and
     73  7cb6							; can be any value.
     74  7cb6							; The end of the release phase is encoded by a 0.
     75  7cb6				   tt_InsFreqVolTable
     76  7cb6							; 0: Pizzicato bassb
     77  7cb6		       8a 8a 89 88*	      dc.b	$8a, $8a, $89, $88, $86, $85, $85, $84
     78  7cbe		       83 00 83 83*	      dc.b	$83, $00, $83, $83, $83, $00
     79  7cc4							; 1+2: Square2
     80  7cc4		       8c 8c 8b 89*	      dc.b	$8c, $8c, $8b, $89, $87, $85, $84, $83
     81  7ccc		       82 82 81 81*	      dc.b	$82, $82, $81, $81, $81, $00, $81, $00
     82  7cd4							; 3+4: Square
     83  7cd4		       85 85 85 85*	      dc.b	$85, $85, $85, $85, $84, $83, $83, $82
     84  7cdc		       82 82 81 81*	      dc.b	$82, $82, $81, $81, $81, $81, $00, $80
     85  7ce4		       00		      dc.b	$00
     86  7ce5
     87  7ce5
     88  7ce5
     89  7ce5							; =====================================================================
     90  7ce5							; Percussion instrument definitions (up to 15)
     91  7ce5							;
     92  7ce5							; Each percussion instrument is defined by:
     93  7ce5							; - tt_PercIndexes: The index of the first percussion frame as defined
     94  7ce5							;	 in tt_PercFreqTable and tt_PercCtrlVolTable
     95  7ce5							; - tt_PercFreqTable: The AUDF frequency value
     96  7ce5							; - tt_PercCtrlVolTable: The AUDV volume and AUDC values
     97  7ce5							; =====================================================================
     98  7ce5
     99  7ce5							; Indexes into percussion definitions signifying the first frame for
    100  7ce5							; each percussion in tt_PercFreqTable.
    101  7ce5							; Caution: Values are stored with an implicit +1 modifier! To get the
    102  7ce5							; real index, subtract 1.
    103  7ce5				   tt_PercIndexes
    104  7ce5		       01 0a 0c 	      dc.b	$01, $0a, $0c
    105  7ce8
    106  7ce8
    107  7ce8							; The AUDF frequency values for the percussion instruments.
    108  7ce8							; If the second to last value is negative (>=128), it means it's an
    109  7ce8							; "overlay" percussion, i.e. the player fetches the next instrument note
    110  7ce8							; immediately and starts it in the sustain phase next frame. (Needs
    111  7ce8							; TT_USE_OVERLAY)
    112  7ce8				   tt_PercFreqTable
    113  7ce8							; 0: Kick
    114  7ce8		       00 01 02 03*	      dc.b	$00, $01, $02, $03, $04, $05, $06, $87
    115  7cf0		       00		      dc.b	$00
    116  7cf1							; 1: HH
    117  7cf1		       80 00		      dc.b	$80, $00
    118  7cf3							; 2: Snare
    119  7cf3		       01 03 06 0e*	      dc.b	$01, $03, $06, $0e, $13, $11, $15, $14
    120  7cfb		       17 1b 00 	      dc.b	$17, $1b, $00
    121  7cfe
    122  7cfe
    123  7cfe							; The AUDCx and AUDVx volume values for the percussion instruments.
    124  7cfe							; - Bits 7..4: AUDC value
    125  7cfe							; - Bits 3..0: AUDV value
    126  7cfe							; 0 means end of percussion data.
    127  7cfe				   tt_PercCtrlVolTable
    128  7cfe							; 0: Kick
    129  7cfe		       ee ed ed eb*	      dc.b	$ee, $ed, $ed, $eb, $e9, $e8, $e8, $e6
    130  7d06		       00		      dc.b	$00
    131  7d07							; 1: HH
    132  7d07		       87 00		      dc.b	$87, $00
    133  7d09							; 2: Snare
    134  7d09		       8b 8a 8a 8a*	      dc.b	$8b, $8a, $8a, $8a, $8a, $8a, $89, $88
    135  7d11		       87 86 00 	      dc.b	$87, $86, $00
    136  7d14
    137  7d14
    138  7d14
    139  7d14							; =====================================================================
    140  7d14							; Track definition
    141  7d14							; The track is defined by:
    142  7d14							; - tt_PatternX (X=0, 1, ...): Pattern definitions
    143  7d14							; - tt_PatternPtrLo/Hi: Pointers to the tt_PatternX tables, serving
    144  7d14							;	 as index values
    145  7d14							; - tt_SequenceTable: The order in which the patterns should be played,
    146  7d14							;	 i.e. indexes into tt_PatternPtrLo/Hi. Contains the sequences
    147  7d14							;	 for all channels and sub-tracks. The variables
    148  7d14							;	 tt_cur_pat_index_c0/1 hold an index into tt_SequenceTable for
    149  7d14							;	 each channel.
    150  7d14							;
    151  7d14							; So tt_SequenceTable holds indexes into tt_PatternPtrLo/Hi, which
    152  7d14							; in turn point to pattern definitions (tt_PatternX) in which the notes
    153  7d14							; to play are specified.
    154  7d14							; =====================================================================
    155  7d14
    156  7d14							; ---------------------------------------------------------------------
    157  7d14							; Pattern definitions, one table per pattern. tt_cur_note_index_c0/1
    158  7d14							; hold the index values into these tables for the current pattern
    159  7d14							; played in channel 0 and 1.
    160  7d14							;
    161  7d14							; A pattern is a sequence of notes (one byte per note) ending with a 0.
    162  7d14							; A note can be either:
    163  7d14							; - Pause: Put melodic instrument into release. Must only follow a
    164  7d14							;	 melodic instrument.
    165  7d14							; - Hold: Continue to play last note (or silence). Default "empty" note.
    166  7d14							; - Slide (needs TT_USE_SLIDE): Adjust frequency of last melodic note
    167  7d14							;	 by -7..+7 and keep playing it
    168  7d14							; - Play new note with melodic instrument
    169  7d14							; - Play new note with percussion instrument
    170  7d14							; - End of pattern
    171  7d14							;
    172  7d14							; A note is defined by:
    173  7d14							; - Bits 7..5: 1-7 means play melodic instrument 1-7 with a new note
    174  7d14							;	 and frequency in bits 4..0. If bits 7..5 are 0, bits 4..0 are
    175  7d14							;	 defined as:
    176  7d14							;	 - 0: End of pattern
    177  7d14							;	 - [1..15]: Slide -7..+7 (needs TT_USE_SLIDE)
    178  7d14							;	 - 8: Hold
    179  7d14							;	 - 16: Pause
    180  7d14							;	 - [17..31]: Play percussion instrument 1..15
    181  7d14							;
    182  7d14							; The tracker must ensure that a pause only follows a melodic
    183  7d14							; instrument or a hold/slide.
    184  7d14							; ---------------------------------------------------------------------
    185  7d14		       00 1f	   TT_FREQ_MASK =	%00011111
    186  7d14		       00 08	   TT_INS_HOLD =	8
    187  7d14		       00 10	   TT_INS_PAUSE =	16
    188  7d14		       00 11	   TT_FIRST_PERC =	17
    189  7d14
    190  7d14							; Intro left
    191  7d14				   tt_pattern0
    192  7d14		       11 08 3e 08*	      dc.b	$11, $08, $3e, $08, $12, $3e, $3e, $08
    193  7d1c		       13 08 3e 08*	      dc.b	$13, $08, $3e, $08, $12, $3e, $3e, $08
    194  7d24		       11 08 3e 08*	      dc.b	$11, $08, $3e, $08, $12, $3e, $12, $3e
    195  7d2c		       13 08 3e 08*	      dc.b	$13, $08, $3e, $08, $12, $3e, $13, $08
    196  7d34		       00		      dc.b	$00
    197  7d35
    198  7d35							; Intro2 L
    199  7d35				   tt_pattern1
    200  7d35		       11 08 34 08*	      dc.b	$11, $08, $34, $08, $12, $34, $34, $08
    201  7d3d		       13 08 34 08*	      dc.b	$13, $08, $34, $08, $12, $34, $34, $08
    202  7d45		       11 08 34 08*	      dc.b	$11, $08, $34, $08, $12, $34, $12, $34
    203  7d4d		       13 08 34 08*	      dc.b	$13, $08, $34, $08, $12, $34, $13, $08
    204  7d55		       00		      dc.b	$00
    205  7d56
    206  7d56							; Intro2-fill L
    207  7d56				   tt_pattern2
    208  7d56		       11 08 34 08*	      dc.b	$11, $08, $34, $08, $12, $34, $34, $08
    209  7d5e		       13 08 34 08*	      dc.b	$13, $08, $34, $08, $12, $34, $34, $08
    210  7d66		       11 08 34 08*	      dc.b	$11, $08, $34, $08, $12, $34, $12, $34
    211  7d6e		       13 08 34 08*	      dc.b	$13, $08, $34, $08, $12, $34, $13, $08
    212  7d76		       00		      dc.b	$00
    213  7d77
    214  7d77							; Intro right
    215  7d77				   tt_pattern3
    216  7d77		       6f 08 73 08*	      dc.b	$6f, $08, $73, $08, $6e, $08, $73, $08
    217  7d7f		       6f 08 73 08*	      dc.b	$6f, $08, $73, $08, $73, $08, $73, $08
    218  7d87		       6f 08 73 08*	      dc.b	$6f, $08, $73, $08, $6e, $08, $b3, $08
    219  7d8f		       6f 08 73 08*	      dc.b	$6f, $08, $73, $08, $b3, $08, $73, $08
    220  7d97		       00		      dc.b	$00
    221  7d98
    222  7d98							; Intro2 R
    223  7d98				   tt_pattern4
    224  7d98		       71 08 73 08*	      dc.b	$71, $08, $73, $08, $74, $08, $71, $08
    225  7da0		       6f 08 73 08*	      dc.b	$6f, $08, $73, $08, $b3, $08, $73, $08
    226  7da8		       b3 08 73 08*	      dc.b	$b3, $08, $73, $08, $b3, $08, $73, $08
    227  7db0		       71 08 73 08*	      dc.b	$71, $08, $73, $08, $74, $08, $71, $08
    228  7db8		       00		      dc.b	$00
    229  7db9
    230  7db9
    231  7db9
    232  7db9
    233  7db9							; Individual pattern speeds (needs TT_GLOBAL_SPEED = 0).
    234  7db9							; Each byte encodes the speed of one pattern in the order
    235  7db9							; of the tt_PatternPtr tables below.
    236  7db9							; If TT_USE_FUNKTEMPO is 1, then the low nibble encodes
    237  7db9							; the even speed and the high nibble the odd speed.
    238  7db9				  -	      IF	TT_GLOBAL_SPEED = 0
    239  7db9				  -tt_PatternSpeeds
    240  7db9				  -%%PATTERNSPEEDS%%
    241  7db9					      ENDIF
    242  7db9
    243  7db9
    244  7db9							; ---------------------------------------------------------------------
    245  7db9							; Pattern pointers look-up table.
    246  7db9							; ---------------------------------------------------------------------
    247  7db9				   tt_PatternPtrLo
    248  7db9		       14 35 56 77	      dc.b	<tt_pattern0, <tt_pattern1, <tt_pattern2, <tt_pattern3
    249  7dbd		       98		      dc.b	<tt_pattern4
    250  7dbe				   tt_PatternPtrHi
    251  7dbe		       fd fd fd fd	      dc.b	>tt_pattern0, >tt_pattern1, >tt_pattern2, >tt_pattern3
    252  7dc2		       fd		      dc.b	>tt_pattern4
    253  7dc3
    254  7dc3
    255  7dc3							; ---------------------------------------------------------------------
    256  7dc3							; Pattern sequence table. Each byte is an index into the
    257  7dc3							; tt_PatternPtrLo/Hi tables where the pointers to the pattern
    258  7dc3							; definitions can be found. When a pattern has been played completely,
    259  7dc3							; the next byte from this table is used to get the address of the next
    260  7dc3							; pattern to play. tt_cur_pat_index_c0/1 hold the current index values
    261  7dc3							; into this table for channels 0 and 1.
    262  7dc3							; If TT_USE_GOTO is used, a value >=128 denotes a goto to the pattern
    263  7dc3							; number encoded in bits 6..0 (i.e. value AND %01111111).
    264  7dc3							; ---------------------------------------------------------------------
    265  7dc3				   tt_SequenceTable
    266  7dc3							; ---------- Channel 0 ----------
    267  7dc3		       00 00 01 02*	      dc.b	$00, $00, $01, $02, $80
    268  7dc8
    269  7dc8
    270  7dc8							; ---------- Channel 1 ----------
    271  7dc8		       03 04 03 04*	      dc.b	$03, $04, $03, $04, $85
    272  7dcd
    273  7dcd
 Track size:  $12b
    274  7dcd					      echo	"Track size: ", *-tt_TrackDataStart
